River Embankment Restoration Project Statistics

(Nanjing) Statistics for river embankment restoration projects, with the Dongzhuang in Shandong, the Zhongxiang breach closing in Hubei, and the Huangbei River guiding into the sea in northern Jiangsu projects being the largest. The Dongzhuang breach closing cost approximately 2.6 million yuan, the Zhongxiang dike repair cost over 2 million yuan, and the Huangbei River guiding into the sea project cost approximately 3.6 million yuan. Other dike restorations totaled approximately 2 million yuan, making a total of approximately 11 million yuan. These funds were allocated by the central government, and in addition to a portion of cash, it is also necessary to issue a certain amount of disaster relief public bonds. The amount will be determined after consultation with Minister Kong. The Economic Commission originally intended to convene a meeting of relevant agencies to discuss the embankment restoration plan, but because the plans proposed by the two water conservancy associations have been discussed separately with the competent authorities, it is not intended to hold a meeting. Furthermore, the Huangbei River guiding into the sea project is of great importance to the lives and properties of various counties in northern Jiangsu. The Economic Commission advocates completing the project within three to five months to divert the Huang River into the sea and reduce flooding. After the funds are decided within a few days, the commission can discuss the implementation with the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Huang River Guiding Association, recruit a large number of workers, and expedite the project into the sea, aiming to complete the project between May and June next year. Jiangxi Provincial Administrative Commissioner Conference

Proposals Divided into Four Groups: Civil Affairs, Finance, Construction, and Education. Baojia, Schools, and Rural Areas are the Focus of Discussion

Nanchang correspondence. In order to reorganize the Baojia system, strengthen organizations, and promote various important policies, the provincial government specially convened a conference of administrative inspectors from various districts. The opening was originally scheduled for the 21st, but due to the aviation exercises on the 22nd and 23rd, it was changed to the 24th. At 8:00 AM on this day, it was held at the provincial government. Provincial Government Chairman Xiong Shihui, the four department heads of Civil Affairs, Finance, Construction, and Education, and administrative commissioners from the first to the eighth districts, Wei Suzhong, Shao Hongji, Lin Jing, and others, numbering more than ten people, attended. After the ceremonial salutations, Xiong Shihui reported on the general prevalence of the Baojia system, common shortcomings, and various aspects that should be reformed. Subsequently, various commissioners reported and expressed their opinions separately. Then, the concrete plan for the Baojia system was discussed. In the afternoon, the proposals were categorized and discussed in groups on the 25th. The Civil Affairs Group was chaired by Wang Youyong, the head of the Civil Affairs Department, and held at the Civil Affairs Department. The secretary of the department also participated. The main points were to organize the public to investigate the population, determine the Baojia organization, implement the Baojia public agreement, and promote all important policies. The Finance Group was held at the Finance Department and was chaired by Director Wu. The secretary of the department also participated. The discussion focused on the unified planning and expenditure of Baojia funds, improving land taxes, reorganizing land, implementing budgets and final accounts, and eliminating all financial abuses. The Construction Group was convened by Director Gong and held at the Construction Department. The main points of discussion were road construction, water conservancy construction, rural revival, cooperative promotion, and various construction problems related to corvée labor. The Education Group was convened by Director Cheng and held at the Education Department. The main points of discussion were the establishment of Baojia schools, the promotion of free education, the training of the public, and the promotion of the New Life Movement, etc. The above proposals all took the Baojia system as the central point. On the 26th, two general meetings were held to review the various cases examined by Groups 1, 2, 3, and 4 and submit reports. Regarding the Baojia aspect, the key points decided were to improve the Baojia organization, carefully select Baojia personnel, and improve the status of Baojia chiefs. Regarding funding, unified collection and expenditure were implemented. The goal was to reach 15 million yuan for the annual three Bao (Baojia, Bao schools, Bao health) funding. The central work was to integrate "management," "education," "nurturing," and "hygiene" to improve the level of the people's group. It is said that there are still many proposals to be discussed and decided, and the conference was extended by one day on the 27th for discussion and closed on that day.

Guanyun Various Circles Appeal for the Speedy Opening of Baiqian and Other Dams

To Avoid Water Congestion and Prevent the Collapse of the East Bank of the Yanhai River. The County Government Indulges the Landlords' Requests and Abandons the West Bank.

Guanyun correspondence. This year's Yellow River flooding has severely affected the Haishu area. The vicinity of Banpu has become a marshland. The Xinpu-Banpu highway is now several feet deep in water, and transportation relies entirely on shipping. Currently, various circles in Guanyun are firmly requesting the authorities to open the Liuli Baiqian and other dams to avoid water congestion and expansion of the disaster area. On the 24th of this month, another urgent telegram was sent to the provincial government, which is recorded as follows: "Most Urgent. Zhenjiang Provincial Government Chairman Chen, Civil Affairs Department Director Yu, Construction Department Director Shen, Provincial Party Department Gentlemen, This year's Yellow River flooding has already caused disasters on the west bank of the Yanhai River in Guanyun, with water depths varying from three, four, five, six, seven, to eight feet. Fields, houses, and graves have collapsed almost completely, and many people and livestock have also died. The water level is rising sharply day by day, and the east bank of the Yanhai River and the county seat are in imminent danger. It has been verified that during major floods, the people are allowed to freely open the Liuli Baitui Niudun Three Dams according to regulations. The water situation is extremely dangerous. Two-thirds of the Niudun and Liuli dams have been opened, but the Baiqian dam is completely blocked, causing water to become congested. The county seat is surrounded by water, and the Huaibei Salt Affairs Inspection Sub-Office and the Xinban highway are also several feet deep in water. Appeals have been made repeatedly to the Administrative Inspector of the East China Sea District and the Guanyun County Government to request the opening of the Liuli Baiqian Niudun Three Dams. The Commissioner granted permission and instructed to open the dams. However, Magistrate Xu Xiekuo went to the province on official business, and the section chief, at the request of the large landowners in the southeast, refused to open the Liuli and other dams, citing unwillingness to expand the disaster area, abandoned the west bank of the Yanhai River, protected the fertile land on the east bank, and built the Yanhai Dike to resist the flood. The construction of the Yanhai Dike is merely a waste of financial resources. It has been verified that water flows downward, and water control is based on dredging, and never on water storage. Moreover, the agricultural work on the east bank of the Yanhai River has been completed. Drawing water into the sea not only does not hinder anything but can also eliminate pests. If the water is congested for a long time, the east bank of the Yanhai River may also collapse. If a river is blocked, it will break, and many people will be injured. The sowing of wheat will be delayed indefinitely. In the future, the downward flow of fresh water will also affect the spring sweeping of the salt merchants, which will affect national taxes and the people's livelihood, which is by no means insignificant. In addition to sending a telegram separately, we are compelled to respectfully request your review and approval to order Magistrate Xu Xiekuo of Guanyun County to open the Liuli Baiqian Niudun Three Dams day and night, and also to order the opening of more channels to the sea to facilitate drainage and relieve the county. We are extremely anxious and await your orders."

Liu Bingzhong Talks About the Engineering Situation and Water Conditions at Dongzhuang

The Collapse and Water Seepage of the Geliang Does Not Affect the Breach Closing Project

Kaifeng correspondence. Liu Bingzhong, the inspection director of the Henan, Shandong, and Hebei Flood Control Office, went to inspect the water conditions and engineering situation in the Dongzhuang breach area and returned to Bian yesterday. According to his talk: (1) After the Jiangsu Dam, a new ramp should be built, although it is a direct hit, the river surface is wider, and the ramp has slowed down slightly. (3) Li Shengtun has built five sections of revetment, wing walls, and sweeping. Three sections have become submerged in the water. The first section has been protected with stone to level the slope. According to Director Zhang, the inner part can be built again after the completion of the more than 100-zhang revetment along the river. (4) The south end of the Geliang was scoured, eroded, seeped water, and collapsed into an opening, measuring 130-140 zhang wide. The length of the embankment at the south end where it connects to the levee is about 40 zhang, and the length of the embankment at the north end is estimated to be about 300 zhang. A total of 25 sections of straw sweeping have been built on the north end near the water seepage area. The work is still guarded by Yucheng adding compartments. Although the large surge directly injected into the sweeping section a few days ago, it flowed south along the sweeping and still poured out from under the dam of the sixth breach. Therefore, the water seeping out of Geliang is clear water without surge until before the retreat embankment. The deepest point along the levee is more than one meter, and the north end is about one or two inches. The people of the county are rushing to build a revetment in front of the embankment foot to prevent wind and waves. After eating the Geliang, the terrain of the north section is higher than the south section. Although the south section is seeping water, the direction of the surge has not moved north. This is also due to the nature of the downward-flowing water. Therefore, according to the current situation, although the Geliang has collapsed and seeps water, it has no effect on the breach closing project plan. (5) There are more than 1,600 cubic meters of stone material currently in stock, and stone-carrying boats are still arriving at the work site every day. There is very little straw material, and it is being urged to purchase. As for the dangerous works in the cold stockade area of the second and third sections in southern Hebei, they are no longer collapsing, and the situation is easing. (27th)

The Largest Bridge on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway is Completed

Contracted by Shanghai Dachang Company

According to the Central News Agency, the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway has a 1,700-foot steel bridge structure in the Liangjiadu area of Nanchang, with two railway tracks and two highway lanes on top. It is the first railway and highway combined bridge in China, completely designed and built by Chinese engineers. Construction began in November of last year and has now been fully completed. Trains can be run as soon as the railway is completely laid. The cost of the bridge is 860,000 yuan, and the contractor is the Shanghai Dachang Construction Company. Due to the extremely deep excavation of the piers, the company and the engineers of the railway bureau encountered various special engineering difficulties during the major flood in Jiangxi this year before the project was completed. The bridge project is entirely self-made by the Chinese people, and this bridge should be considered the beginning. The above picture is a photograph taken during the construction of the bridge.

Guangdong Province's Construction Public Bonds are Mortgaged to Shanghai Banks

Half of the public bonds, 2.5 million, are used as collateral. Chen Zhongbi is Scheduled to Come to Shanghai in a Few Days to Continue Negotiations.

In order to develop industry, Guangdong Province is preparing to issue 5 million yuan in construction public bonds. They are now scheduled to be issued on December 1st of this year. The face value of the public bonds is divided into four types: 5 yuan, 10 yuan, 50 yuan, and 100 yuan. It is also planned to promote the mortgage of half of the public bonds to Shanghai banking circles to borrow money. Feng Rui, the director of the Agricultural and Forestry Bureau of Guangdong Province, and Chen Zhongbi, the president of the Guangzhou Municipal Bank, once came to Shanghai to contact various banks. A Xin Xin News Agency reporter learned from banking circles yesterday that Chen Shenbi, the president of the Guangzhou Municipal Bank, is scheduled to come to Shanghai again in a few days to continue negotiations on mortgage loans with banking circles. The Shanghai banks have already expressed their approval in principle and agreed to assist with the loan. Therefore, President Chen's visit to Shanghai this time will involve further consultations. The amount of the loan, the term, the interest rate, etc., can all be negotiated at that time, and then a contract will be signed on a regular basis.

According to Industrial News, the regulations for issuing bonds have been submitted for approval, and they are recorded as follows: (1) Purpose: to expand the sugar, soda, sulfuric acid, textile, fertilizer, paper, and beverage factories in Guangdong Province and prepare for the Wengjiang Hydroelectric Plant. (2) Amount: 5 million yuan. (3) Interest rate: 7% per annum. (4) Guarantee: the operating surplus of the Xicun Cement Factory in Guangdong Province will be used as a fund, and a fund management committee will be organized to allocate the factory's surplus to the committee on a monthly basis for special storage and use. The Guangdong Provincial Bank will be designated as the agency for managing the repayment of principal and interest. (5) Repayment period: from May of the 25th year of the Republic of China to November of the 29th year of the Republic of China, repayable in five years. The organizational regulations for the Public Bond Fund Management Committee have designated Qu Fangpu, the director of the Department of Finance, and others to draft them, and Chen Yuanying, Chen Zhongbi, Hu Jixian, Shen Zaihe, etc., are internally designated as committee members, with Qu Fangpu serving as the chairman of the committee.

Economic Inspection Delegation to Japan, Yu Tang, etc., Returned to China Yesterday

Wu Daquan Expected to Arrive in Shanghai on the 2nd of Next Month

(Central News Agency) Our country's economic inspection delegation to Japan has completed its inspection of industry and commerce in that country. Except for Chen Guangfu and others, who have already returned to China, yesterday, additional delegation members Yu Zuoting, Tang Shoumin, and four others, along with commissioner Qin Kai and seven others, returned to China aboard the Shanghai Maru. Prominent figures from the financial sector, such as Zhang Peishen, welcomed them at the pier. The delegation leader, Wu Daquan, and his party are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 2nd of next month. A detailed account of their arrival and conversations is provided below:

Returned to Shanghai Yesterday: Our country's economic inspection delegation to Japan, led by delegation leader Wu Daquan, crossed the sea to Japan on the 6th of this month. They landed in Nagasaki and proceeded to Kobe, Osaka, and other central industrial and commercial areas of Japan to visit various economic cooperatives in that country. After completing the group inspection schedule on the 23rd, each delegation member continued with independent visits. Delegation members Tang Shoumin, Yu Zuoting, Liu Hongsheng, Huang Wenzhi, commissioner Qin Kai, Li Zhishi, Li Beitao, secretary Zhou Xijing, Gu Jiemei, and ten others returned to China together yesterday aboard the Shanghai Maru, landing at the Huishan Wharf at approximately 3:00 PM.

Welcome from Relatives and Friends: Those who went to the wharf to welcome them yesterday included approximately 50 people, including Zhang Peishen of the Bank of Communications, Zheng Chengqing of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Yu Qiaqing of the Shipping Association, Xu Zhiyi of the China Merchants Bureau, He Molin, Chen Weiqing, and relatives and friends. As each delegation member disembarked, they shook hands and chatted happily with their relatives and friends. They then changed to cars and returned to their residences to rest.

Written Conversations: While on board, the reporter met with delegation member Yu Zuoting and inquired about the journey and his impressions. He presented the written conversations of the delegation members, stating that after the economic inspection delegation to Japan arrived in Japan, from Nagasaki, to Kobe, Osaka, Nagoya, and the two capitals, they received warm hospitality from the local industrial and commercial sectors. They exchanged opinions with a sincere attitude, all agreeing that Sino-Japanese amity requires mutual understanding to complement each other's strengths and weaknesses. Mutual assistance leads to mutual benefit, and mutual benefit initiates amity. China is rich in natural resources and should base its nation on agriculture, forestry, and mining. Japan, through decades of effort, has become an industrial nation, aggressively competing in global commerce, but lacks raw materials and needs to rely on external supplies. Therefore, there is a relationship between China and Japan, and cooperation is necessary. However, cooperation should be based on equality and mutual specialization, and one-sided demands rarely succeed. During this inspection tour, banquets and discussions repeatedly conveyed this idea, which was well understood by the Japanese. However, a country is an entire organism, and the economy is the lifeline of the organism. All aspects of a country, including politics and military affairs, are related to the economy. Therefore, economic cooperation is essentially a comprehensive cooperation between the two countries. Merely talking about the economy is insufficient. It is hoped that people from both countries will enhance all aspects of their relationship through economic ties, so that this inspection will not have been in vain.

Yu's Impressions: Mr. Yu continued to describe his impressions of the trip, saying that he followed the entire delegation and visited famous places, and his reflections can be summarized in several points: 1. Since the Meiji Restoration, Japan has studied and imitated material civilization, and it seems to have entered a period of creation today. Judging from the progress, it should not be difficult to surpass European and American countries in the future. 2. The entire nation, whether officials or common people, shows the spirit of hard work and bearing heavy burdens like the Germans after the war. 3. The entire nation is diligent, thrifty, hardworking, and maintains the humility of the East, and education is widespread, making it easy to receive organized training. This is the reason why all industries and businesses in the country are well-organized. 4. Historical concepts are still deeply rooted in the people, and the government also protects them in many ways. Religious belief and material civilization are progressing simultaneously, which maintains much of the social morality and public sentiment and should not be ignored. As for initiating and organizing the Sino-Japanese Trade Association, it is based on the above-mentioned concepts, hoping to realize economic cooperation between China and Japan, similar to the established Sino-American Trade Association. Preparations for the association have already begun. As for other details, Delegation Leader Wu will provide a detailed report to the public upon his return to China in the coming days.

More Arrivals to Come: The delegation members currently still in Japan include delegation leader Wu Yuanquan, Zou Minchu, Zhou Zuomin, Huang Jiangquan, Zhong E, Shang Kui, Zhu Shugang, Secretary-General Liu Tiecheng, commissioners, and staff members. It is reported that they will return to China in batches. Delegation Leader Wu and others are scheduled to leave Japan on the Nagasaki Maru tomorrow (the 31st) and are expected to arrive in Shanghai on the afternoon of the 2nd of next month.

Chinese Ratepayers Association Publishes Opinions on Valuation and Collection of Rates; The Rent Valuation Committee Has No Legal Basis; Its Judgments Are Not Binding Externally

The Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession issued "Opinions on the Shanghai Municipal Council's Valuation and Collection of Municipal Rates", which stated, "According to the Land Regulations of the Yangjingbang, the standard for calculating the Municipal Rates, commonly known as the police rates, can be based on the valuation agreed upon by the Council and the property owner. The reason why the regulations stipulated this way was to accommodate the actual situation at the time, that is, only those who owned and used their own property and did not rent it out. Although it has been revised many times, this provision remains the same. However, in practice, for a time, the Council still conducted rent valuation and rate collection for rented houses, but it was the same as the current land valuation, which was often below the actual rent. Therefore, rate collectors often manipulated things to sacrifice public revenue to enrich their own pockets. Subsequently, the Council's move to increase the rate was met with opposition, and this kind of shady deal gradually became clear. In order to increase revenue, the actual rent was used as the standard for rate collection. Therefore, rate collectors must present rent receipts to new residents when collecting rates. If there are any fabrications, in addition to checking the landlord's accounts, they will also sue in court. There have been precedents to follow. Since then, the Council's practice of using the actual rent as the basis for rates on rented houses has become a strong convention, and it is in line with facts and principles. Therefore, this convention can occur, and public opinion is unanimous without any objection. The above-mentioned estimation behavior of the regulations can only be applied to those who own and use their own property. In 1927, the Council increased the rate from 14% to 16%, which was met with strong opposition. Although it was still paid under protest, it was reduced by two percentage points after the sale of the Electricity Department in 1929. Since then, the Council has repeatedly sought to increase it, but it has not dared to implement it due to the decline in the local economy and mixed public opinion. Therefore, it wanted to use the rent valuation method, which had become a dead letter, to increase rate revenue in fact. For example, if the rent is 100 yuan, the monthly rate should be 14 yuan based on a 14% rate. If the valuation is increased to 150 yuan, the rate must be 21 yuan. The rest can be deduced by analogy. The rate has not increased, but the rate has increased by one and a half times, which is equivalent to increasing the rate from 14% to 21%. The Council also thought that this plan would be considered too arbitrary, so it claimed that it was convenient for taxpayers to appeal and set up the so-called 'Rent Valuation Committee'. Its purpose was to be like the 'Property Committee', both of which are public decision-making bodies, so that their judgments are equivalent to the final judgment of the court. In fact, the organization, personnel selection, and election method of the Property Committee are stipulated in the Land Regulations of the Yangjingbang. The Committee has no legal basis, and its establishment is only approved by the Board of Directors as a consulting body for the Finance Committee. The Committee itself has no legal basis, and its judgments have no binding force. Taxpayers are allowed to arbitrarily increase the rate of Municipal Rate Collection by the Council, originally because any change in the rate must be agreed upon by the taxpayers before it can be implemented. If the Council can arbitrarily increase the rate for those who have actual rent to rely on, the Council can arbitrarily increase rate revenue at any time without obtaining the consent of the taxpayers. Then the taxpayer's control over the Council is completely lost, and the spiritual foundation of the Public Concession's Municipal Government is fundamentally shaken. Based on the above, the Association has always given serious opposition to the Council's valuation of the Municipal Rate Collection without regard to actual rent, and adheres to the following principles: (1) The Council should collect rates based on the actual rent for houses with actual rent, and may use rent valuation to collect rates for those who own and use their own property. (2) The Council's establishment of the so-called Rent Valuation Committee has no legal basis and does not recognize its right to hear lawsuits according to law. Its judgments have absolutely no external binding force. (3) The Council shall not arbitrarily increase rate revenue. Unless the taxpayers agree to change the rate, the taxpayers have the absolute right to refuse to pay the Council's extra-legal rate revenue. Gold Exchange Notice: Sellers Must Pay Special Security Deposits."

Although Gold Market Prices Are Stable, Jia Tai Gold Shop Closes

Gold Exchange Notice: Sellers Must Pay Special Security Deposits

(Huadong News Agency) Since several brokerage firms, such as Xie Da Xiang on the 23rd of this month and Yuan Kang Xiang on the 25th, temporarily closed due to margin issues, brokers have been wary of large-scale trading. On the afternoon of the 28th, Jia Tai Broker No. 133 was also closed due to a margin issue. The Gold Exchange issued Notice No. 2108 yesterday morning, stating that Jia Tai Gold Shop's margin has not been cleared and should be temporarily suspended from business. Afterwards, the Huadong News Agency reporter investigated from all parties and learned that the shop was established four years ago with a capital of more than 60,000 yuan. It was a limited shareholder company with a manager named Lu. The current debt is about 40,000 yuan.

Sellers Pay Additional Special Security Deposits

Previously, due to extraordinary market fluctuations, a special security deposit of 50 yuan per bar was collected from buyers, which was implemented from the 27th. Yesterday, Notice No. 2106 was issued, stating that due to extraordinary market fluctuations, gold trading in the Exchange will, in accordance with the provisions of Article 42, Paragraph 2 of the Exchange's Business Rules, require sellers to pay additional special security deposits of 50 yuan per silver coin from today onwards.

Brand Name Guarantee Requires Prepayment of Security Deposits

Another Notice No. 2107 stated that gold shops using brand names to guarantee shares and using them as security deposits in the Exchange will, due to extraordinary market fluctuations, be required to prepay security deposits if purchases and sales exceed 70 bars or more before they can increase trading. American Asian Airline to Launch Next Month

Hong Kong as the Final Stop Not Yet Confirmed

(Central News Agency) United Airlines of America has been planning to develop Far East transportation and open the American Asian Airline for a long time, and it is scheduled to launch next month. Its starting point is San Francisco in the United States, and the final destination in Asia was originally planned to land in Hong Kong. However, the reciprocal conditions with the British government have not been agreed upon. Later, it was planned to directly reach Guangzhou, but our country did not approve it due to sovereignty relations. Finally, it was agreed with Portugal to take Macau as the final destination, and it was scheduled to launch the San Francisco to Manila section next month. As for Manila to Macau, due to business relations, it is feared that the losses will be too great, so it is temporarily postponed. Recently, it was heard that the United Kingdom and the United States have recently signed an aviation agreement. The United Kingdom has allowed Hong Kong to be the final stop of the line, and the United States has granted the Atlantic aviation rights in exchange. The reporter inquired with the United Airlines Company in this city yesterday, and it was said that they had not heard of this news. The various rumors are probably not true. The vice president, Mr. Bixby, is still in the Philippines and is expected to come to Shanghai next month. In short, due to business relations, the American Philippines section will be launched first.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Announces Answers to Stamp Tax Questions

Totaling 26 Items

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, in order to answer questions about stamp tax application, had previously compiled a special publication on the Stamp Tax Law, which was published by the Commercial Monthly and was very convenient for merchants to refer to. Later, because of various questions that needed to be submitted to the Ministry for verification, a total of 25 verified replies were published in the ninth issue of the Commercial Monthly. It is now reported that the Chamber of Commerce has recently published 26 items in the tenth issue of the Commercial Monthly, including: (1) Explain the difference between organizational and total organizations, and the scope of internal documents; (2) Stamp application methods for construction factory report documents, etc.; (3) Salary books should be stamped; (4) Verify the stamp application questions for construction account books and delivery slips; (5) Labor contracts for workers do not need to be stamped; (6) Sales report forms should be stamped according to the current asset account books; (7) Stamp application methods for construction factory subcontracting account statements and detailed valuation sheets, etc.; (8) Stamp tax standards for dye tickets and lost insurance tickets; (9) Ministry-approved overdue account statements are not absolutely limited to the New Year; (10) Official contract papers for buying and selling fields and houses do not need to be stamped; (11) The Ministry-approved tax rate for ship's bills of lading cannot be changed before the Legislative Yuan revises it; (12) Verify the stamp application method for pharmacy order invoices; (13) Rent receipts under 10 yuan are exempt from stamp tax; (14) Land lease books should be stamped with two cents each year; (15) Old lease books before the implementation of the new law are not stamped annually; (16) Milk company diary cards are internal audit documents and do not need to be stamped; (17) People's petitions do not need to be stamped; (18) Ministry-approved car tickets do not need to be stamped; (19) Ministry-approved documents used internally are made into booklets and should be stamped according to law; (20) Banks acting as agents for national treasury bonds are exempt from stamp tax; (21) Triplicate invoice stubs do not need to be stamped; (22) Distribution lists should be stamped according to the document for taking out goods; (23) Color lists of knitting factories can be renamed as original and duplicate invoices; (24) Ministry-approved liquor licenses do not need to be stamped; (25) Membership certificates are not stamped; (26) Account statements in the form of letters should also be stamped.

Factory Registration in This City: Stamp Duty on Certificates Changed to One Yuan

Registered factories do not need to re-register, but must pay the certificate fee and apply for a certificate.

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau is handling factory registration. Previously, in accordance with Article 6 of the revised Factory Registration Rules of the Ministry of Industries, a stamp tax of two jiao was required for factory registration certificates. Now, the bureau, based on an instruction from the Municipal Government, relayed a communication from the Ministry of Industries stating, "In accordance with the revised Article 6 of the Factory Registration Rules of the new Stamp Tax Law of the Ministry of Finance, the stamp tax has been changed to one yuan, and the matter has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for review and record, and notices have been sent to other departments for their information." Therefore, the bureau has issued an order to the Social Affairs Bureau to announce the correction. Furthermore, factories that have already been approved for registration do not need to re-register. The details are listed below, and the original text of the bureau's announcement is recorded as follows:

Social Announcement: The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau announced, "According to Instruction No. 16057 from the Municipal Government on October 28, 'According to Communication No. 13681 from the Ministry of Industries, "The revised Factory Registration Rules and the form of the registration certificate were previously communicated to your Municipal Government for reference and implementation. Article 6 of the rules stipulates that a stamp tax of two jiao is required for the registration certificate. The reason for this tax rate is that the spirit of factory registration lies in the submission of the two types of registration forms, A and B, in Article 3 of the rules, so as to understand their business operations and exercise supervisory powers. The function of the certificate is only to prove that the factory has been registered, so as to avoid the penalties of Article 11 of the rules. It is completely different from the licenses of company registration and the certificates of business registration, which are used to obtain rights. There is no specific provision for the tax rate for stamp tax in the various categories of Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations on Stamp Tax. Therefore, it is handled by analogy to Article 3, Category 21, "Application for Certificate of Naturalization," which is set at two jiao. Now that the Stamp Tax Law has been formulated and promulgated and ordered to be implemented from September 1935, Article 16 of the law, which is attached to the tax rate table 35, does not contain the certificate and similar certificates. Tax rules, resulting in the tax rate of the previous factory registration certificate, no basis, after all, can the certificate be exempted from using stamp tax? Regarding the tax rules, after consulting the Ministry of Finance Yecheng, 'Check the Stamp Tax Law, the various licenses and certificates related to the business that should pay stamp tax, is to distinguish whether to levy donations and taxes, in the tax rate table brother thirty-one section backup questions, industry is detailed in the record, the factory registration and the company registration and business registration, the matter is the same, and its registration and registration certificates, etc., are only charged the certificate fee, and are not issued in accordance with the levy of taxes and donations, this factory registration certificate, according to law, should be affixed with stamps, (and so on, should be in accordance with the provisions of Article 6 of the Stamp Tax Law, Tax Rate Table 32, the original factory registration certificate of the fixed stamp tax of two corners, changed to one yuan, in addition to the factory registration rules Article 6 amended, changed to stamp tax of one yuan, and submitted to the Executive Yuan for review and record, and issued separately, corresponding to the investigation, transfer order to comply with, to the various places before receiving this amendment tax rate official documents, all the factories that have been registered to receive the certificate, still affixed according to the original tax rate, no longer affixed, so as to avoid confusion, and hope to check and order to know the lotus, etc.准准此、合行令仰該局即便知照、等因奉此、合亟布吿、仰本市各工廠一體周知、自二十九日起、登記憑單之印花稅、應遵照部令、改貼一元、連憑單費一元、共為二元、此布

Receiving the certificate.

Also, a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency inquired and learned that factories in this city that have been approved for registration in accordance with the Factory Registration Rules in the past only need to pay the certificate fee and stamp tax to the local competent authority to receive the certificate in accordance with the provisions of Article 6 of the revised Factory Registration Rules of the Ministry of Industries. There is no need to re-register, so you can go to the Social Affairs Bureau to pay the certificate fee and stamp tax to receive the certificate again, without having to re-register.

Two Ships, "Xin Ping" and "Hua Xin," Encountered Danger

One Collided and Damaged in the Huangpu River, One Aground in Haizhou and Difficult to Save

Xin Ping Damaged: The "Xin Ping" ship of the Taiping Steamship Company was carrying a large amount of coal from Pukou to Shanghai for unloading. It entered the port at 11:45 am yesterday and berthed on buoys No. 28 and No. 29 in the Huangpu River, preparing to unload the coal into barges. When the ship was docking, more than a dozen barges scrambled to block the unloading. Barge No. 13317 of Heji Company rushed towards the left outer side of the ship, intending to take the lead. Unexpectedly, the forward movement was too aggressive, and the suspended ladder on the outer side of the Xin Ping ship was damaged, and the hull was also damaged, causing heavy losses. After the accident, the Taiping Shipping Company notified the insurance company and informed Heji Company. The Xin Ping ship is now unloading the cargo.

Hua Xin Difficult to Tow: The "Hua Xin" ship of the Hua Xin Steamship Company, with a deadweight of more than 3,000 tons, ran aground in Haizhou on the 19th of this month. The shipowner was unable to get out of danger and telegraphed to Shanghai for help. The company received the news and urgently consulted with Jardine Matheson & Co. to send a tugboat to Haizhou for rescue. By 5 pm yesterday, the company received another telegram from Haizhou, saying that the Hua Xin ship had a draft of 19 feet, and the grounding site was only 14 feet deep. After the Jardine Matheson tugboat arrived in Haizhou, it towed it quickly, but it has been going on for three days. Due to the deep grounding, the hull was submerged in the sand and mud to a depth of five feet, resulting in a hundred plans and no way to rescue it. The Jardine Matheson tugboat has decided to return to Shanghai, and the Hua Xin Company is looking for other ways to rescue it, but the towing fee has been sacrificed for 4,000 to 5,000 yuan.

Sun Fucai Plots to Frame His Brother-in-Law, Disregarding the Destruction of His Mother's Corpse, Reports to the Police That His Brother-in-Law Killed His Mother, the Exquisite Armor is a Knife Wound

Sun Fucai from Ningbo, aged [ ], also known as Chu Jiu, came to Shanghai with his mother, Jin, aged 58, on September 11 and stayed at his brother-in-law Xin Xingkuan's place in Ningbo at No. 89 Mike Tor Road, looking for business. Recently, his mother was frightened and became ill, lying in bed. Xin was working as a clerk in Jardine Matheson & Co. His income was not high, and he had a large family, which was not enough to cover expenses, so he could not afford to hire a doctor to treat his mother-in-law's illness. He sought the help of gods and Buddhas, only asking for immortal prescriptions to drink. Sun Fucai was very dissatisfied. Unexpectedly, his mother died at 5 pm the day before yesterday. Sun happened to be out and did not return until 8 pm. Seeing that his mother had closed her eyes and was sleeping soundly, he felt extremely resentful and came up with a plan to add to Xin Xingkuan's experience of prison. He took advantage of the gap to use a small knife to stab a hole in the right abdomen of his mother's body, and secretly went to Dongxi Huade to throw the knife into a river. He went to the Hongkou Police Station to report that his mother was stabbed in the abdomen by his brother-in-law Xin Xingkuan and died, requesting justice. The police chief sent Detective Zhu Jihuang and Detective Bai Mingfu to secretly investigate and learned that Sun had accumulated resentment and made false accusations. He was detained and sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, detailed the previous situation and said that Sun had admitted it in the police station. Sun Jin's body has been in the funeral home on Fei Lun Road waiting for an autopsy. Now, according to Article 247, Paragraph 1 and Article 251 of the Criminal Law, the crime of infringing on the body and making false accusations is prosecuted, requesting [ ] to be detained. Then, according to Xin Xingkuan and his wife Sun, the defendant borrowed money unsuccessfully and accumulated grudges, and came up with this poisonous plan. When questioned, Sun's confession was hesitant. Judge Jiang ruled that he should be detained and rescheduled for review. And Sun Jin's body was clearly dissected by forensic doctors Wei and Zhang. The knife wound was stabbed after death. After Prosecutor Guo Wei lived in the office, he obtained the dead Sun Jin, female, who died of illness before her death. Sun Chu Jiu has been prosecuted by the police and should be sent to court for investigation. The body was handed over to his daughter Xin Sun for a settlement to be taken back for burial.

Creditors of the Hong Kong National Bank's Shanghai Branch Petition to Declare the Shanghai Branch Bankrupt, Petitioner Liang Botang is Given a Deadline to Submit a Power of Attorney, the Respondent Claims That the Assets and Liabilities are Sufficient to Pay Off

The head office of the Hong Kong National Bank is located in Hong Kong and is registered with the British government, while the Shanghai branch is also located on Jiangxi Road. In August of this year, the Hong Kong head office ceased operations, and the Shanghai branch was also ordered to announce its cessation of operations on September 16. At the same time, the shareholders' meeting and the creditors' meeting of the Hong Kong head office recommended Lu Zhongqing, Ma Huibi, and Ma Antu as liquidators of the Shanghai branch, and the Ministry of Finance also approved the creditors' request and appointed Lu Zhongqing as the supervisor and liquidator of the Shanghai branch. Recently, Liang Botang, the chairman of the creditors' group of the Hong Kong National Bank's Shanghai branch, hired a lawyer to petition the Shanghai branch of the bank to be declared bankrupt in accordance with Article 1, Paragraph 2 of the Bankruptcy Law, "If the debtor stops payment, it is presumed that it is unable to pay" and Articles 2 and 58 of the same law and the First Special District Court. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Jiang Guanjin opened the 13th Court for summons. Lu Zhongqing, the legal representative of the respondent, hired lawyer Huang Zongdong to appear in court to defend, and raised a preliminary issue, saying that whether the creditors' group was indeed entrusted by the creditors, if it could not enter these two proofs, the court should dismiss the petitioner's petition. The petitioner's lawyer immediately replied that Liang Botang was the standing committee member and chairman elected by the creditors' meeting, authorized by the creditors, but there was no power of attorney, but it could be corrected according to law. The court ruled that the power of attorney should be submitted to the court within two days, otherwise the petition would be dismissed. Then, the petitioner's lawyer stated the reasons for the petition, saying that the creditor of the Shanghai branch of the Hong Kong National Bank requested the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to investigate its legal person status from the British Consulate. Then, Director Yu replied that the British Consul considered that the bank was opened by Chinese joint venture and registered with the Chinese Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and should be considered a Chinese legal person, and Lu Zhongqing was the manager of the Shanghai branch and was an interested party with the bank. According to the law, he could not be a liquidator. Now that he could not pay, he asked to declare him bankrupt according to the bankruptcy law. According to Huang Zongdong's lawyer, although the Shanghai branch of the Hong Kong National Bank was registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, foreigners can register with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce when operating businesses in Jiangsu. It is presumed that it is indeed a Chinese legal person. According to the Bankruptcy Law, the main business place must be located, and the main business place of the respondent is in Hong Kong, and Shanghai is only a branch. As for Lu Zhongqing's election as a liquidator, it was elected by the shareholders' meeting and the creditors' meeting, which fully complied with the provisions of the Company Law, and the assets of the Shanghai branch, in addition to the profit-making assets, exceeded the amount of liabilities, which was not the inability to pay debts as defined by the Bankruptcy Law. It should be rejected in accordance with the provisions of Article 63 of the Bankruptcy Law. The petitioner's petition was rejected, and the accountant's asset-liability report, account books, and registration certificate of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce were submitted to the case for inspection. Judge Jiang checked the report and ordered both parties to withdraw and await the ruling.

The Lake Society Holds a Group Wedding for Fellow Townsmen, the First is Scheduled to be Held on New Year's Day Next Year, Registration of Married Persons Has Now Begun, the Wedding Rules Have Been Officially Announced

The Shanghai Guizhou Road Lake Society has launched a group wedding for fellow townsmen in the Lake area in order to promote frugal weddings. The date of the first event has been set for New Year's Day next year, and registration for married persons has now begun. The Datong News Agency reporter now explores and records the details as follows:

Notice to Fellow Townsmen

Since the Shanghai Municipal Government initiated the new lifestyle group wedding, it has been in line with the purpose of frugal weddings. Various places have followed suit one after another. People in our Lake area have always advocated frugality. Later, the world's customs were bad, and the wedding ceremony became extravagant. Waste is not spent. That is, the etiquette is reciprocal, competing for the victory of the door, unnecessary consumption, not one by one. In order to seek innovation and frugality, the company plans to hold the first group wedding for fellow townsmen on New Year's Day next year. However, the matter is unprecedented, and everything depends on the group's support to facilitate promotion. Therefore, we have set up a method and sent letters to solicit them. We hope that you will check and, if you have any introductions, please fill in the report at the company before November 30 in accordance with the prescribed procedures so that we can start preparing. I have always known that Taiduan is happy to support fellow townsmen's business, and will definitely be happy to support it. Sincerely, the Lake Society Committee.

Participation Rules

Lake Society held a group wedding rules for fellow townsmen, (1) Qualification for participation All fellow townsmen from the six counties in the Lake area can apply to participate in the group wedding, regardless of whether one of the man or woman is a fellow townsman. (2) Number of times held, each spring, summer, autumn and winter seasons each year, one time each, the date will be determined and announced at any time. (3) Place of holding, in the company's auditorium, and the chairman of the company and the chairman of the executive committee will be the officiant. (4) Participation fee Participants should pay 16 yuan per couple, and there are no other fees. (5) Application registration Applicants should first apply to the company and fill in the application form, and then the company will issue a registration certificate, and participate with the certificate when the deadline arrives. (6) Compliance with the time, all participants should follow the following, "Notes on Group Wedding" in addition to the items, all the time for the wedding ceremony should be strictly observed. (7) Marriage certificate, prepared and issued by the company. (8) Supplementary provisions, all those who have registered and withdraw halfway will not be refunded the fees paid.

Notes on Wedding

Notes on participating in the group wedding, (1) Participants should first ask the company for an application form, fill in each item in ink regular script in accordance with the prescribed format. (2) Men and women who are married must prepare one and a half-inch portrait photo of each person, affixed to the application form. (3) The parents or guardians of the applicant, and the officiant, must sign and seal. (4) The applicant must personally seal. (5) After filling in the application form, the applicant must bring the participation fee in person to the company for registration and issue a registration certificate. (6) All those who register to participate should be one week before the wedding ceremony, the officiants of both men and women, and the introducer, come to the company with the married person and seal the marriage book. (7) When getting married, the bride and groom must wear regular formal clothes and veils of the prescribed color sample. The formal clothes are undertaken by the crepe industry association and can be contacted with the company's staff for handling. (8) The groom must wear black socks and black leather shoes, and the bride must wear white gloves and shoes and socks of the same color as the formal clothes. The shoes are made of plain satin, and the heels should not be too high. (9) The bride must not let her hair down. (10) When getting married, the bride holds a bouquet of flowers, which is prepared by the company on behalf of the company, so as to be consistent. (The price is paid by the participants according to the payment.) (11) The wedding time is scheduled for 3 pm, and the married person should arrive at the company one hour in advance. If they are not there after the deadline, it will be regarded as a waiver. (The fees collected will not be refunded.) (12) No bridesmaids and veil-carrying children are allowed. (13) When performing the ceremony, except for the married person and the four officiants from both sides, all others must enter the auditorium with viewing tickets. (14) The viewing tickets in the preceding paragraph are issued by the company and the registration certificate when the marriage book is sealed.

According to Xin Xin News Agency, before the China Public Yellow Car Company closed down, it issued bad checks to the Shanghai Finance Bureau to pay car taxes and obtain temporary car permits, intending to save the bad luck by taking advantage of the opening of the Sixth National Games. Unexpectedly, it failed to do so, and the Finance Bureau held the check, and the payment was not available. After several negotiations, it was politely requested to postpone it for a few days. The Finance Bureau also took into account the economic downturn in the market to sympathize with the commercial difficulties and approved its request. Unexpectedly, after the closing of the conference, the company immediately announced liquidation, especially since it was unable to pay the publicity donation. It is said that the Finance Bureau, for the sake of national taxation, cannot allow it to be cunning. In addition to entrusting the bureau's legal counsel Jiang Hechun to pursue the matter according to law, it also requested the authorities to give priority to the right to obtain it.

The Words "Robber" are Tattooed on the Face, the Tattooing Case is Judged, Zhang Guoqing is Sentenced to Two Years and Six Months

During the half night on the 2nd of September in the Bao Fan Workshop opened by Zhang Guoqing, a native of Yangzhou, at No. 36 of No. 46 Jian, Tianbao Road, Zhabei, a thief, Teng Shunzi (also a native of Yangzhou), took advantage of the opportunity to break in and attempt to steal. Zhang Guoqing noticed and captured Teng, and together with his friends Wang Dacheng and Wang Maojun, used a rope to tie Teng to a pillar and subjected him to tattooing. He used a long needle to tattoo the words "Robber" on the left side of Teng's face and applied blue ink. Then, he released him. Teng suffered this lifelong humiliation and could not accept it. He reported the incident to the police and arrested Zhang Guoqing, Wang Dacheng, and Wang Maojun together with Teng Shunzi and sent them to the local court. Prosecutor Zhang Zi interrogated them and filed separate lawsuits in the Criminal Court. Judge Wu Xiangzu held a hearing and concluded the trial, waiting for sentencing. Now, it is known that the case was sentenced by Judge Wu in court at 11 am yesterday. He ordered the four defendants, Zhang Guoqing, Wang Dacheng, Wang Maojun, and Teng Shunzi, who were in custody, to be brought to the case and asked about their age and place of origin one by one. He stood up in court and announced the sentence (main text). Zhang Guoqing injured the body of another person and was sentenced to three months of fixed-term imprisonment. The defendants refused to accept the verdict and declared an appeal. The interrogator ordered them to state the reasons and appeal according to law. The defendants were taken back into custody.

Zhang Xinying Establishes the Far East Library, Accused of Fraud; the Envelope's Upper Corner is Printed with a Magnificent Building; It's the New Building of the Guohua Bank on Henan Road; Many Deceived People are Reporting to the Police

Zhang Xinying, from Lianzhou, originally worked as a manager at a certain dance hall. Suddenly, at No. 66 Mou'er Road, she rented a vacant house to establish the Far East Library, soliciting business by sending out a flood of letters to various locations both locally and abroad. After receiving remittances from people to purchase books, Zhang would embezzle the funds without sending the books. People then realized she was using a false name to defraud them, and they sent letters to the General Inspectorate to report her. The detective chief dispatched Gao Xian'gen, a detective from the Political Department, to work with Ding Huaguo, a detective from the relevant Xin Zha district police station, to conduct a thorough investigation and collect the original letters she had sent. Upon inspection, they determined that Zhang was indeed intentionally committing fraud. On the upper corner of the front of the envelopes used by the Far East Library, she had printed a magnificent building, claiming it was the library's address, while the back featured a system chart of the library's internal organization, with no fewer than ten departments, including a novel editing department, a magazine editing department, and an English translation department. Each department was labeled with a telephone number. This exaggerated technique was designed to mislead people into believing the library was sound and grand. In reality, the image of the library's address was the building of the Guohua Bank on Henan Road, and the so-called internal organization was purely fabricated. The two detectives returned to investigate a few days ago and found that Zhang had moved the Far East Library's sign to No. 7, Lane 161, Baike Road. They inquired with the sub-landlord of the house, who said that Zhang had only rented a front wing room, and upon inspecting the books for sale inside, they found only a few volumes. This further convinced them that she was running a fake bookstore to swindle money without a doubt. Therefore, Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer from the Public Concession, filed a lawsuit against Zhang Xinying in the First Special District Court on charges of fraud. Yesterday morning, Judge Liu Yugui held a hearing, but the defendant did not appear. A lawyer appeared on her behalf, saying that the defendant had gone to Hangzhou and had not returned, and requested a postponement. Judge Liu then ordered the hearing to be rescheduled for Thursday.

Strange Hat-Snatching Case: Zhang Danjie, Does He Have Special Tendencies? Song Daniu's Intentions Are Revealed by His Words

The Public Concession police yesterday morning at 9:30 escorted the suspect, Song Daniu, a 21-year-old from Anhui, to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court, requesting detention in accordance with Articles 76 and 101 of the Criminal Procedure Law. Zhang Tianyin, the Public Concession police's lawyer, rose and stated the reasons for the detention, saying that at 8:30 last night, Constable No. 12 of the Public Concession police was on duty at the intersection of North Zhejiang Road and Tiantong Road when he suddenly heard loud shouts from the Yizhong, a public cemetery, of the Tongren Fuyuan Hall behind the court. He went to investigate and saw a crowd gathered. The person being petitioned in this case was standing to the side, and an elderly man was lying on a rickshaw, appearing to be seriously injured. The constable questioned the elderly man, who said his name was Zhang Danjie, 52 years old, and that Song Daniu had snatched his hat and pushed him over during the ensuing argument, injuring his buttocks. Consequently, Song, Zhang, were taken to the police station. Zhang was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment, and the doctor found that Zhang's injuries were quite severe, with a fractured pelvis, so he was kept in the hospital for treatment. However, the suspect, Song Daniu, said something completely different at the police station, saying that he knew Zhang Danjie because he was a hawker selling spiced beans at the rooftop garden of the New World Company, and Zhang would come to play there, so they knew each other. Two weeks ago, Zhang invited Song to leave the New World Company and go to the China Hotel on Zhejiang Road, where Zhang opened a room and asked Song to perform a homosexual act, after which Zhang gave Song one yuan. Last night, they met again at the New World Company, and Zhang again invited Song to go to the China Hotel for more fun, but when they reached the entrance of the hotel, Zhang suddenly didn't want to go inside and wanted to find a more secluded path, so they went to the Yizhong area on North Zhejiang Road, intending to make Song do something immoral. Song refused, leading to an argument, and Zhang was pushed to the ground, etc. The police said that the statements of the two parties conflicted, and they did not have time to investigate in detail, so they requested that Song be detained, and the doctor should examine Zhang to see if he had such characteristics. When questioned, Song Daniu said, "He asked me to commit sodomy once and would give me one yuan. Last night, he invited me to the Yizhong, Zhang touched my lower part with his hand, kissed my face, and hugged me. I threw him down, causing him to fall to the ground," etc. Judge Liu Yugui examined the statements and ordered Song to be detained for seven days for further questioning.

Lu Bingkui, a Hangzhou native who worked as a wind instrument player, lived at No. 493 Guangdong Road. Yesterday morning, Chief Judge Feng Shide opened the First Criminal Court to continue the hearing. Regarding the defendant's claim that the deceased had injured himself by bumping into a protruding corner of the counter, the inspection revealed that it was impossible. The deceased's wife, Chen Zhu, hired lawyer Yu Bing to appear in court and filed a civil suit, requesting that the defendant be ordered to pay a one-time payment of 3,000 yuan for living expenses and 500 yuan for funeral expenses, as she had a 70-year-old great-aunt and young children to support, all of whom depended on the deceased for survival. After further arguments between the police lawyer Wang Yaotang and the defendant's lawyer, Judge Feng announced the conclusion and scheduled the verdict for Thursday morning.

Plagued by Poverty and Illness, Fortune Teller Ran Zi Ran; Stabbed Himself in the Chest with a Sharp Knife; Fatally Wounded and Died

Ling Mingyue, a 47-year-old from Anhui, currently residing on the mezzanine floor of No. 240 Xin Xin Li, Jin Shenfu Road, French Concession, had been unemployed for a long time and now made a living by setting up a fortune-telling stall. His wife, Ling Ye, 42 years old, lived with her maternal family at No. 108 in the same lane. They had two sons, the elder of whom had come of age and joined the army, but had been missing for many years with no news. The younger son was still an infant. Ling suffered from stomach pain, which led to a smoking addiction. His stomach pain would recur intermittently. Recently, due to economic pressure, his old illness often recurred, and he had no money for treatment, leading him to have suicidal thoughts. At 11:30 PM on the 28th, taking advantage of the fact that a certain Jia, a fruit vendor who lived with him on the mezzanine, was asleep, Ling took Jia's three-inch-long sharp knife used for cutting fruit and stabbed himself in the chest. Blood gushed out, and he fell to the ground. Jia was awakened by a noise in his sleep and was shocked to see Ling lying in a pool of blood. He called out to his neighbors and urgently reported it to the Central Police Station. An ambulance arrived and took Ling to Guangci Hospital, but because the wound was fatal, he died after two hours despite treatment. The hospital notified the police, who transported the body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch for autopsy. At noon that day, prosecutor Wang Ren from the Second Special Court, along with forensic doctor Wei and clerk Peng, arrived at the scene. They determined that the deceased had died from a knife wound sustained before death. Guan Ju questioned Ling's wife, Ling Ye, and then ordered the body to be released to her for funeral arrangements.

Customs: Tongsha Lightship Enters Dock for Repairs

The Tongsha lightship, which belongs to the Jianghai Customs and is moored in the South Channel of the Yangtze River import route, has been in disrepair for many years, and many of its internal parts have been damaged. Therefore, the Customs has specifically revoked it and replaced it with another lightship, issuing a notice stating: "The Tongsha lightship, which belongs to the Jianghai Customs and is moored in the South Channel of the Yangtze River import route, now needs to enter the dock for repairs and should be temporarily revoked and replaced with another lightship. The details are listed below for the information of merchants and others." The details are as follows: A. Details of the temporary lightship: (1) Lightship style: The ship is painted red and has no name on either side. Once the Tongsha lightship is repaired, it will be sailed back to its original location, and the temporary lightship will be revoked without further notice. (2) Lighting situation: The ship is equipped with a fourth-order lens white fixed light, flashing once every 17 seconds, i.e., bright for 12 seconds and dark for 5 seconds. It can be seen within 11 nautical miles in clear weather. (3) Fog warning equipment: The ship is also equipped with a fog mirror, ringing a bell every 15 seconds to warn in dense fog or cloudy weather. (4) Mooring situation: The ship hangs a white mooring light from sunset to sunrise, 12 feet above the deck, to indicate the direction of the ship's mooring. B. Date of revocation: Tentatively scheduled for around November 5 of this year, at which time no further notice will be given. C. Related charts: Charts No. 50 and 1011 of the Hydrological Chart of the Ministry of the Navy of the Republic of China.

National Coarse Grain Merchants Establish Federation: Firmly Request the Abolition of Bran Tax; Promote Cheng Xin and Others to Petition the Sixth Plenary Session; Oil Factories Resolve to Sacrifice Business Collectively

Representatives from various local coarse grain and oil cake industry groups and factory transport merchants held a joint meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday at the coarse grain market on Minguo Road to establish the National Manufacturers' Association for Requesting the Abolition of Bran Tax. They elected representatives Cheng Xin and six others to go to Beijing to petition the Sixth Plenary Session. The details are as follows:

Establishment of National Manufacturers' Association

Various local coarse grain and oil cake manufacturers, in view of the imposition of additional bran tax in Guangdong Province, which increases the burden on farmers and merchants, have jointly implemented a business suspension and transport strike to strive for its cancellation. They have persisted for two months, but have not yet achieved results. In order to plan for long-term struggle and unify forces, representatives from various local areas held a joint meeting at the third floor of the coarse grain market on Minguo Road yesterday afternoon. More than seventy people attended, and they elected Gu Xin Yi as chairman and Kong Ru Lin as secretary, establishing the National Coarse Grain and Oil Cake Industry Association for Requesting the Abolition of Additional Bran Tax and Property Tax in Guangdong Province. They elected (Shantou) Rao Dongdao, Liu Liugu, (Guangdong) Fang Yusheng, (Zhenjiang) He Xianggu, (Hankou) Xie Boqin, Chen Shide, (Qingdao) Huang Hongji, (Xuzhou) Zong Minglun, (Bengbu) Li Peisheng, (Wuxi) Jiang Hongbin, (Shanghai) Gu Xinyi, Chen Ziheng, Zhu Jingan, Zhang Lunqing, He Quansheng, Cao Xigeng, Cai Yukun, and twenty-one others as committee members, and began operations immediately. Representatives from Kaifeng and Jinan will also rush to Shanghai to participate in the coming days.

Petitioning the Sixth Plenary Session in Beijing

The Sixth Plenary Session is scheduled to open in Beijing on November 1. Local members of the Central Committee are traveling to Beijing together to attend. In order to strive for the cancellation of the bran tax and make all members of the Central Committee aware of the plight of farmers and merchants, representatives from manufacturers in Shanghai, Qingdao, Bengbu, Xuzhou, and other places, Gu Xinyi, Chen Ziheng, Chen Zenan, Zhu Jingan, and seven others, were elected as representatives to form a petition group to go to Beijing to petition the Sixth Plenary Session. Local manufacturers have also scheduled to hold a joint expanded petition during the Fifth National Congress on November 11.

The Shanghai Oil Factory Trade Association held an emergency meeting at its office at No. 105 Jiangxi Road at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. More than twenty people attended, including (Shunyu) Zhu Jingan, (Changde) Chen Ziheng, (Suifeng) He Quansheng, (Dadexin) Cao Xigeng, (Dayoubao) Zhang Lunqing, (Tongsheng) Xue Chengzhang, (Changji) Tan Jinglan, (Lide) Zhang Xiande, and Jiang Hongbin, representative of Wuxi Hengderunfeng Factory. Chairman Zhu Jingan presided over the meeting. First, standing committee member Chen Ziheng reported on the progress of the struggle against the bran tax, and then it was resolved that if Guangdong Province does not abolish the bran tax, they will collectively sacrifice their business.

Page 11

Thoroughly Rectify Local Bands; Municipal Government Announces Measures to Ban Disorderly Performances

The Municipal Government previously believed that the music played by local bands was indistinguishable between joyful and mourning tunes, and was disorderly and chaotic, with joyful music played at funerals, or light and frivolous music played at solemn and grand commemorative ceremonies. This not only violated the meaning of the music, but was also inappropriate and ridiculous. Therefore, the "Measures for Banning Disorderly Performances by Shanghai Bands" were specifically formulated and approved by the Municipal Government at its recent 391st Municipal Affairs Meeting according to the review opinions. Yesterday, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau was specifically instructed to implement them. The reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency reports the banning measures as follows: "Measures for Banning Disorderly Performances by Shanghai Bands" Article 1: All bands in this city that are for commercial purposes shall abide by these measures. Article 2: The bands mentioned in these measures refer to bands that use brass instruments. Article 3: Bands in this city shall comply with the colors and styles specified by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for band flags and road performers' clothing. Article 4: No band in this city shall use music scores that have not been reviewed and approved. Article 5: When hired, all bands in this city shall play appropriate music based on the nature of the ceremony being held, and shall not play joyful music at funerals or be disorderly and chaotic. They shall also listen to the instructions of inspectors or supervisors. Article 6: Any band in this city that violates the provisions of Article 3 shall be subject to a fine of up to 20 yuan. Article 7: Any band in this city that violates the provisions of Article 4 or Article 5 of these measures may have its registration certificate revoked. Article 8: Any band in this city that operates without registering with the Social Affairs Bureau, or any registered band that violates the provisions of these measures and continues to operate after its registration certificate has been revoked, shall be subject to a fine of up to 20 yuan for each offense. Article 9: After the registration certificate of any band in this city has been revoked, the Social Affairs Bureau shall promptly notify the Public Security Bureau of the band's name and address, instructing them to be aware. Article 10: The Public Security Bureau shall promptly forward to the Social Affairs Bureau for review and handling any violations by any band of the provisions of Article 3, Article 4, Article 5, Article 6, or Article 8 of these measures. Article 11: Any matters not covered in these measures may be amended at any time upon request. Article 12: These measures shall take effect from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Government.

Six Buddhist Organizations Solicit Opinions on Casting a Giant Bell; Dispatch Li Jingxu and Shen Hanfu to Survey the Mountain; Models of the Giant Bell and Bell Tower Begin to Be Displayed

Six organizations in this port, including the Buddhist Laymen's Forest, Buddhist Bookstore, Buddhist Pure Land Society, Chinese Buddhist Association, Jiuhua Buddhist Association, and Shanghai Buddhist Association, have launched a campaign to cast a giant Far Eastern bell. According to the news from the bell preparation office, it has officially begun. The details are as follows:

Resurveying the Mountain

The bell preparation office also sent the monk Juechun to Jiuhua Mountain to select a base on the peak. According to the monk's letter, he has selected several scenic locations on Lanluan Mountain. He requested that personnel be sent to the mountain to survey and purchase one for the construction of the bell tower. After receiving the letter, the preparation office dispatched preparation committee members Li Jingwei and Shen Binhan to the mountain to select a site the night before last.

Spectacular Models

The bell is specified to weigh 18,000 kilograms and be cast from pure copper, engraved with the entire Ksitigarbha Sutra, and named the "Underworld Bell." Two models have been cast by Shen Yuanji Foundry in this port. One model, which is quite spectacular, is currently on display at the Buddhist Laymen's Forest. A model of the bell tower has also been made, divided into three floors, which is particularly elegant and solemn. It has also begun to be displayed at the Laymen's Forest.

Soliciting Opinions

In order to solicit opinions on casting the bell, the preparation office has issued a notice stating: "The casting of the Jiuhua Mountain Underworld Bell is imminent. However, the materials to be used are still difficult to determine. Some say to mix seven parts of purple copper with three parts of brass. Some say to buy old sounding copper and recast it, which is not only cheaper, but also more reliable in terms of sound. Some say to mix copper and iron, which produces a better sound than copper. There are many ways to cast the bell and use materials. It is impossible to decide which is the most appropriate. This matter is important and must be carefully considered. Which material is the most suitable, and how should it be combined to achieve the purpose of a loud and far-reaching sound, so that it does not fail the original intention of casting the bell this time? We hope that you will not hesitate to teach us and provide detailed guidance."

White Lotus Creek Port – Lao Gongmao Shipyard Fire

At the Lao Gongmao Shipyard, a Chinese-owned factory in the White Lotus Creek Port of Pudong, a fire broke out at 7:30 yesterday morning. The fire started in the cold working area, where workers were using tools on a wooden structure with a lead sheet roof. When flames were noticed, desperate attempts were made to extinguish the fire, but these were ineffective, causing the fire to spread uncontrollably. The factory immediately sent urgent telegrams to various fire departments requesting assistance. Director Zhao of the Pudong District Fire Brigade quickly arrived on the scene with his team in fire engines to assist in the rescue efforts. By this time, the fire was burning fiercely. Two small boats owned by the factory were located under the shed, one named "Jixing," which was being repaired in a dock, and another which was old and unusable. Both boats caught fire simultaneously. As the hulls were mostly made of wood, they were easily combustible. Although several water hoses were used to extinguish the blaze, the boats were completely destroyed. Fortunately, firefighters were able to protect the interior of the cold working area. The fire was completely extinguished after two hours. A wooden shed with an area of fifteen square fathoms and two small boats were destroyed, with losses estimated at over five thousand yuan. According to Mr. Ren, the person in charge of the factory, the fire was caused by a short circuit due to the factory's electrical wiring, which had not been replaced for many years. Turning off the electricity meter was not sufficient to stop the fire. Officer Ju Dai Baoqing of the White Lotus Creek branch police station inspected the scene and prepared a report to be submitted to the Tangqiao police station for forwarding to the General Bureau for review.
