Shanghai Shen Bao Supplement

Commentary

Chen Xianzhou's Antiques Aid Disaster Relief

— Zhang Ji

According to a Hankou dispatch from the Central News Agency on the 24th: Hubei collector Chen Xianzhou is willing to donate more than 4,000 pieces of antiques from his collection, valued at 800,000 yuan, entirely for disaster relief funds. This cannot be said to be a major event in the midst of disaster relief efforts.

This year's floods in various regions are more severe than in the past, but in terms of relief, the government authorities do not have the same overall policy as in previous years. Although civil servants have been ordered to donate salaries to aid disaster relief, the 20 million yuan disaster relief public bond was only approved by the Central Political Conference the day before yesterday and must still be reviewed by the Legislative Yuan. It is uncertain when it will be issued, and it is even more impossible to say when it will reach the hands of the disaster victims. As for the general public, there is no longer the same enthusiasm as in previous years. Variety shows, flower selections, and dance selections are held all day and night, but only 15,000 yuan is sent to the charity association. The film industry uses female stars to appeal, but how much has been raised is not publicly announced. However, it is said that the floor of the ticket office is full of torn-up discount coupons. Although there is a sign in front of the dance hall that says "Dance a little more, save a life," everyone in the dance floor is still reluctant to move forward. The disaster relief swim using mermaids to appeal only attracted more than 1,000 spectators. We do not know how the soccer game went in Shanghai, but in Nanjing it also only attracted more than 1,000 people. Based on past performance, the upcoming total mobilization of boy scouts for disaster relief will not necessarily have surprising results.

Analyzing this phenomenon, most of the reasons are naturally due to the general economic recession in society. People are too busy saving themselves to care about saving others. But the death of the human heart is also evident. Why? Today's social economy is indeed in a recession, but there are still many wealthy families who can remain unaffected by relying on the legacy of their ancestors and current exploitation. However, they are unwilling to pluck a single hair to benefit the world. Is this not evidence of the death of the human heart?

Now, Chen Xianzhou is actually willing to sacrifice all of his more than 4,000 pieces of antiques. In this death of the human heart, this cannot be said to be a glimmer of human light, which can serve as a wake-up call to the general misers! We know that antiques are indeed called "external possessions," but for someone who loves antiques to be willing to donate antiques, especially those worth a huge 800,000 yuan, this cannot be done without a generous and righteous spirit. Therefore, Chen Xianzhou's actions are particularly worthy of our admiration and praise.

Shanghai is a region where talented people gather, and there must be no shortage of antique collectors as rich as Chen Xianzhou, but we have not seen anyone as generous and righteous as Chen Xianzhou. We sincerely hope that people will be inspired by this news and not let him be the only one to excel. We also want to sincerely tell the officials in charge of disaster relief that they should still focus on this aspect and stop focusing on women.

Occupation

— Si

He was awakened from a sweet dream by the alarm clock, and the room was pitch black. He rubbed his sleepy eyes, savoring the illusion in his dream. The pain of life's oppression crawled over his heart like a snake again. He had thought of quitting his current job several times. The salary was so meager that he could not even support himself with the endless work from morning till night. When he received his father's tearful letter from home, he did not have the courage to pick up a pen. Could he even tell his father about this kind of life? And how could he answer his father's wishes?

Grayish-white light had already leaked into the room, symbolizing his own future. He reluctantly got out of bed, turned on the light, and saw his haggard face in the mirror. The tangled thoughts prevented him from indulging in futile fantasies again. People had to live!

When he went out, the sky was covered in white fog, and the road was quiet without a single pedestrian. The morning in the city was desolate enough. Who would get up early if not for profit? Occasionally, he saw a few street cleaners in red vests, bending over,

Page 18

like an old horse that had lost its master's affection. They swept the fallen leaves from the trees with a broom, half-heartedly. However, most of the bald branches had already been wrapped in straw. The branches were preparing for winter, but what about the pitiful street cleaners? They were breathing and shrugging their shoulders, trying to get through this winter that felt like a century!

He bought a few pancakes from a pancake stand at the entrance of the alley to fill his stomach. The owner of the pancake stand was very familiar with him, and always greeted him with a smile. Although he knew that this was a means for the shopkeeper to attract customers, he was still satisfied that there was still warmth in this world. Every day from taking the tram to returning to that narrow cage, was there anyone who saw him as an equal?

He always took the first tram out of the factory. The ticket sellers in the tram were dozing off. They seemed to have gotten used to it, nodding, buying tickets, and each occupying a corner, lowering their heads to enjoy a little more peace and quiet. When he got off at the Bund outside the main road, the clock on the Jianghai Customs Building was already 7:20. He stepped on the pier, where the dew of the night had not yet awakened, and found a small steamer with a red chimney mark. When he saw his colleagues, they nodded to each other, and several of them climbed into the cabin like machines. It seemed a little warmer here. Everyone was smoking or flipping through the day's newspapers. This time was very precious, and after that, they would be beasts of burden for ten hours. The steamer departed at 7:30 and took 45 minutes to reach the factory. But there were exceptions, and it was okay for the foreign foreman to be late, but if an employee missed the steamer, you would sacrifice two days' wages if you did not ask for leave in advance. Although they were also office staff, they were treated the same as workers.

Initially, he saw an advertisement in the newspaper for a typist for this company's Shanghai office. After half a day of exams, he was lucky enough to be selected among dozens of people wanting to snatch the job. But the next day, when he went to the office, the foreign boss ordered him to go to the factory in Pudong. The preferential treatment naturally disappointed him, and his status as a college student was also seen as a piglet, the same as the workers! But people had to live, did he have the courage to refuse this order?

The steamer cut through the thick fog on the river and moved forward at high speed. The sound of the engine was like a hammer hitting everyone's heart in the cabin. Although everyone exchanged warm glances, no one could break the silence. Everyone had a pale face and sluggish movements. During this time, he always looked out at the river, watching the surging tide, watching it bravely crash against the ship's hull wave after wave. Until the steamer turned into the small port, the river became as calm as a mirror, and his heart also calmed down. But the red wall of the tall factory building had already reflected into his eyes from the hold. Looking back, his fellow people, who shared the same fate, were mustering up their energy to prepare to disembark, but he felt tired and unable to move.

Silent Night Market Sounds

— Hua Mu

This place was originally a small market town at its edge. Once night falls, everything becomes even more quiet. The soft sound of fallen plane tree leaves on the roadside, the footsteps and coughs of passersby on the village path outside the fence, can all be heard with extreme clarity. The house happens to be near the main road. Although it is late at night, the only wonton seller in this small town who hawks his wares at night, always knocks his clapper at a fixed time, with a slow and leisurely rhythm, approaching from afar. Every time I hear the unchanging clapper gradually approaching, and then gradually fading away, my mind is filled with a distant longing. I feel that this clapper sound is much more pleasant than the popular songs and music broadcast from the neighbor's radio.

For a long time, I only heard this one and only wonton clapper. In this small town, I didn't find it strange. Until recently, for the past few nights, before the wonton vendor passed by, there was an additional hawker selling sandalwood olives. At first, I couldn't quite make out what he was calling out to sell. I only felt that his three different tones and intonations were filled with a kind of moving and desolate charm. I couldn't resist the lure of this selling voice, and couldn't help but walk to the doorway and look towards the neighboring fence. In the small gap of the fence, a dim lamp quietly leaked in, and a vague figure passed by in a desolate manner.

At that time, I stood at the door, my emotions completely captivated by this illusion. I watched the desolate lamp disappear behind a low wall before returning to my desk, feeling somewhat lost. I regretted why I didn't stop the hawker to see what kind of person he was. Perhaps he was a hunched and weak old man, who might even recount his desolate life to me and exchange it for a few hard-earned copper coins from my hand.

That night, my mood was truly disturbed by that desolate selling voice. Even when I was lying in bed, I felt as if I had lost something, or as if I had done something regrettable behind someone's back. After the wonton clapper passed by with its leisurely sound, this small town seemed to become even more quiet. In particular, the soft sound of the plane tree leaves falling in front of the steps, the distant barking of dogs in the village, and the rustling of the wind, all intermittently emphasized the desolate atmosphere of the silent night in this small town. I have always been indifferent to the autumn wind and autumn rain, rarely experiencing their moving beauty. But this night was different. The autumn night sounds, lamented by sensitive poets and travelers, deeply touched my stubborn heart, perhaps precisely because my mind was constantly dwelling on that selling voice overflowing with desolate charm, and thinking of that pitiful peddler who had to endure hardship for a living in this late night with dew and chilling wind.

Several nights passed like this. I also learned from a child that he was selling sandalwood olives. He even showed me the ones he bought. Judging from their shape, these small, hard things probably didn't have any delicious taste. It also seemed that no one came out to buy them when they heard the hawking. Although I seemed very concerned about this selling voice, I was always limited by habit, and it was usually difficult for me to go out to the entrance to buy snacks from the peddler. Only once, I saw three children surrounding him, and I walked over. A tilted square-framed glass kerosene lamp was placed on one side of the wooden bucket. Inside the wooden bucket was covered with a thick cotton cloth, the color of which was already very dirty and old. The man was squatting next to the wooden bucket, a large hand grabbing a celadon porcelain plate, and scooping downwards, the plate revealing a few dark green olives. A few tender little hands quickly reached out to grab and pick, mixed with the noise of arguing over choosing the smaller or larger ones. After the children dispersed, the man didn't even raise his head, and carried the wooden bucket forward again. I could only stand on the side, silently watching his slightly hunched back, lifting his two thin legs and moving with difficulty in the light of the fire, the three different selling voices filled with desolate charm, again spreading with the night wind on the dark village path...

Until now, every night before the wonton vendor passes by, I can hear this desolate selling voice. Every time I face the lamp alone, the wind and dew are bleak outside, and the dog barks are faint, I can't help but close my book and sigh silently, feeling that the night in this small town is even more terrifyingly lonely.

Autumn Feelings

— Xiu Si

The time when I first had knowledge and feeling about autumn was when I was a primary school student and read Ouyang Xiu's "Ode to the Sound of Autumn." At that time, my understanding of autumn was very simple: the weather is cool, there is a bright Mid-Autumn Festival moon, and there is a southeast wind to fly kites. The climate in the south is close to the tropics. Even in autumn, the trees don't necessarily wither. The beautiful scenery of falling leaves is rarely seen. Therefore, my feeling about autumn is a pleasant mood. What's more, there is the joy of flying kites. (When I came to the north, I had a real feeling about flying kites in the spring, as the primary school textbooks said, "grassy fields, flying kites." In my hometown, I scolded the textbook editors for talking nonsense).

It is said that literati lament autumn because of their suffering and emotions. Although I am also very sensitive, I have not felt sad about autumn in my life. Moreover, in my life, I actually feel happy and joyful about the cool, neither cold nor hot autumn weather.

Others lament autumn, but I love and enjoy it.

My love for autumn when I was young was naturally because I could fly kites. And the kites we flew in the south, in addition to people, birds, insects, and fish, also included a kind that was like a fighter plane, which could fight in the sky. I liked to fly this kind of fighting kite the most. The shape is similar to Japanese kites, but the string used for flying is coated with glass powder using glue, and the manufacturing method is different from others. It can be manipulated freely up and down, left and right in the air. It is not a problem to chase or run away. I feel like I am directing an airplane with radio. It's really interesting. If you feel jealous of those kites that can make sounds, or kites that are not beautiful, no matter how far away she is, if you release your own, turn a somersault, and put your string on her string, release it as much as possible, and use the friction of the glass powder on the string, you will cut her string. Charging left and right, it is simply the prince of the sky. If you unfortunately encounter someone else's fighting kite, then you cannot dominate, and you have to have a duel to the death. When it comes to this duel, it depends on whose glass line is long. The short one loses, which is an irresistible thing. This kind of fighting kite is also like a submarine. The person flying it is not on the grassy field, but standing on their own roof. No one understands where it came from. If the line is long, people several miles away are even more baffled. It's been ten years since I returned to my hometown. I wonder how the children are fighting in the sky in this hometown where the southeast wind is tight! When reading "Dream of the Red Chamber," I found the behavior of the young masters and young ladies in the Grand View Garden to fly kites to drive away bad luck ridiculous; but I developed a combative personality when I was young. I think that should be the reason why I have been running into walls everywhere and achieved nothing over the years?

I don't like the Mid-Autumn Festival moon. But I like to fly my kite on that night when the moonlight is like a painting. Flying a kite at night is really boring without the moon; with the moon, you can see the kite running with the white clouds, and the interest is endless. Some people like to fly kites in the dark night, and listen to its sound. I don't like this. What's the point of only hearing the sound without seeing my kite in the sky? In fact, what I don't like is still because it is dark. Although I am jealous when I hear other people's kites making sounds, I don't know where the kites are, so I can't fly my fighting kites out to show off. Mid-Autumn Festival night is different. The moonlight is like day. Whether it's fighting with people or attacking everyone, you can see everything clearly.

After coming to the north, my understanding and feeling of autumn are different again. The time when my soul was immersed in the embrace of autumn was during the period when I was studying at the foot of Snake Mountain; since I have been rushing around in the world, I have not had that kind of mood. Looking back now, it feels like I am immersed in a dream.

Page 19

Our school had a small park next door, which was the site of Zhang Zhidong's Holding Ice Hall. It was a natural phenomenon for the park to be next to the school, becoming a place for students to stroll and relax. Moreover, it was quiet and secluded, with few tourists, and it also became a place for male and female students to talk about love. In the spring, the park was full of peach blossoms. Upon entering, it was as beautiful as the red glow on the horizon, tempting people to ignite the flames of youth. There were more tourists; in the autumn, the white poplars rustled and moaned at the treetops, and fallen leaves flew all over the ground. The tourists disappeared, and it became the exclusive world of our students. In particular, I liked to walk and sit in the park the most. After walking through the peach tree forest, up a few stone steps, turning behind a large hall with its doors tightly closed, and then going deeper, there were white poplar trees planted all over the hillside under the mountain. Various kinds of chrysanthemums were planted around the thatched pavilion. As long as you sat in the thatched pavilion, your ears could hear the symphony of the white poplars, your eyes could appreciate the chrysanthemums competing to bloom, and you could also look at the white clouds flying in the blue sky—autumn approached you with a fresh and elegant posture, immersing you in her gentle and charming embrace.

What's more, sometimes there were girlfriends to talk to, recite poetry, and sing!

Clouds

— Wei Mang

Clouds are lovely. Look at their ever-changing forms, their colors changing in an instant, lively and exquisite, floating lightly and soaring high. When the wind rolls them, they are like ten thousand horses galloping; when the rain is heavy, they are like a high tide surging. Sometimes they are so delicate, and sometimes they are so magnificent!

Clouds change with the seasons: in spring, they are light and delicate, as tender as a young girl; in summer, they are thick and bold, like a strong man's complexion; in autumn, they are like a simple young woman, lightly made up; in winter, they are like a stern judge, with a cold face, iron-faced and ruthless. People love the clouds of spring and autumn, perhaps because of their admiration for young girls and young women? And their contempt for the clouds of summer and winter, perhaps that is their contempt for the ugly faces of men?

However, there are also people who admire the clouds of summer, such as when the sun sets in the summer and the colorful clouds hang in the west, how strange and varied the dark clouds are! Like people, like beasts, like flowers and plants, like insects and fish: how interesting children find these ever-changing figurative figures! Even those with manly vigor see the summer clouds bringing thunder, and rolling in the timely rain. A gust of wind sweeps past, and dark clouds pour down large droplets of rain. How majestic the scene is, how much it symbolizes a frantic era!

As for the clouds of winter, it seems that no one has ever praised them. Because they are so gloomy, so miserable, so cold and icy, that they create a depressed and melancholy mood in people! The clouds of winter are full of twilight. They are so dull and lifeless that perhaps old people will sympathize with them. As for young people who are full of vigor, how can they feel the same when they see them? In addition, perhaps scientists, moralists with serious faces, and enforcers with no emotions will praise them?

The love of young people for the clouds of spring is not only on the one hand because of their lightness, exquisiteness, liveliness, and loveliness, but perhaps that is also a sign of love? Look at them, gentle and charming, flying over grassy gardens, and gently swaying in the warm spring breeze, floating past the eyes of lovers, and also floating into the hearts of lovers. In that kind of atmosphere, in that kind of environment, a spring cloud floats leisurely in space, how can young people not be intoxicated in the passion of love?

Artists and poets, however, love the clouds of autumn. In movie shots and in art photographs, the clouds of autumn are often captured in the lens. The reason is that the autumn weather is particularly clear, particularly sunny and high. There is no frantic wind, and even the frenzied and miserable appearance is not seen. At this time, the clouds are light, and the edges are often inlaid with pure white silver. The clouds of autumn are colorful and multi-faceted, like charming babies, and like pure and noble women. How can artists not love them? And how can poets not sing about them?

As for the clouds in the rain and the clouds in the high mountains, they are also objects that people love. Look, when the mountain rain is about to come, the clouds quickly fly across the sky, like the galloping of a myriad of troops, and like the dance of a black goddess. And when the rain comes, watching the wandering clouds in the misty rain, that kind of hazy and leaping posture, and that magical realm covered with a black veil, how fascinating and full of mysterious meaning!

The clouds surrounding the mountainside and the thin clouds floating on the mountain peaks have been repeatedly depicted by painters and writers in their writing. Because a pointed mountain is cut into two sections, or a mountain top is crowned with clouds, the image is indeed beautiful and lovable. And because there is a lot of water vapor and trees in the mountains, floating clouds accumulate and fill everywhere, so the valleys and mountain streams, the treetops and stones, are often visited by light floating clouds, making the mountain scenery different morning and evening, and changing in an instant. The beautiful scenery created by white clouds is certainly not comparable to bald little mountains. Otherwise, how could the cloud scenery of Mount Lu be considered a spectacle by people?

Good Youth

Youth are truly the great heroes of the Republic, their attitude unlike others. Young general, his spirit soaring into the sky like a startled swan, graceful as a swimming dragon. Rare is his spirit, knowledge, and insight, all abundant and grand. Good youth, surpassing the masses, although his experience is not deep, and his experience is insufficient, his future hopes are endless.

Youth are truly the great innocent of the Republic, everything appearing light and agile. The number of his transformations are countless, his bones are beautiful and loose, his words are clear and pure. Lovable with uncombed hair and unripened hair, and great ability. Good youth, surpassing the masses, with such a young friend, leading the way, it is not difficult to teach the world.

Youth are truly the good darlings of the Republic, their actions are not silly or dull, one word is straight and only a little bit, entrusting judgment to the public, agile and eloquent. With such innate talent, whether dealing externally or internally, he captures victory on the spot. Good youth, surpassing the masses, even if you have not seen him, only heard his words, it should be greatly enlightening.

Storytelling

Zhu Xiaolin Opening

Xin Sheng (1380) Noon to 1:45 PM

Opening "Retribution Record of a Jealous Woman"

Wang Wen is imprisoned in a dungeon. His wife is concerned and worried day and night. She doesn't understand the meaning of the justice court. Why is there hatred where there is no involvement? It's difficult to bribe the warden. There is no way to get through, lacking a mastermind. A short-lived couple are considerate. They visit to observe the situation. The Diao family's wife is originally a Liu family's daughter. She is the first-class gentleman in Xiangchu. She is a neighbor who can be visited. She is cordial in conversation, warm and kind. She is deeply afraid that the mistress and maid will be jealous. Madame Xu is sad and Madame Liu is embarrassed. She is very anxious and extremely ashamed. Her husband was arrested and taken to be an official. Locked in prison, the matter is not over. I beg you to say a word to your father. It is better than fasting and chanting before the Buddha. If he can be released and return home. I will repay your kindness with grass and a ring in life and death. It is easy to see the father, but difficult to establish connections. He will not leave face for his children. He should go to find another way. I am afraid that the matter will not be successful. Crying and wailing helplessly. Fortunately, the maids around her. Advise her to return to her father's residence in Ningbo. The gentry and officials have half of his friends. The maid is difficult to be free.

Xia Hesheng Three Smiles

Dun Ben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening "Dream of the Red Chamber Lin Daiyu"

A beautiful woman was born in Yangzhou. She does not love joy, but only loves sorrow. She is the lingzhi grass on the banks of the Jiangzhu River. With a devoted heart, she descends to earth to repay tears. The amorous master of Yihong Pavilion. At first sight, their hearts are attracted to each other. They are intimate without hesitation. They are not shy of the affections between close relatives since childhood. Sister and brother, they call out endlessly. It is strange that the mistress of Hengwu is here. Her figure and appearance are as graceful as Concubine Yang. The jade with spiritual powers matches the golden lock. A coincidence that leaves the intention of marriage. She acts that she is generous, frugal, and gentle in nature. Why. The mandarin ducks sit in front of the bed and embroider. Why is it. When the musk skewer the dragon, she is shy. Why is it. Cold fragrance pills, a little maid has a frivolous language. Why is it. The ivory brand game reveals people's flaws. Why is it, her recent actions are more biased. In front of her aunt, she is courteous. She laughs at the oriole skillfully weaving a plum blossom pattern. She wants to weave the pattern so that the heart is set aside by others. Since ancient times, the aunt's relation is closer than the aunt's. This misfortune is always the work of Phoenix Sister. For you, tears flow secretly. For you, I worry when we are apart, and I am shy when we meet. I look forward to a lifelong good match. From there, there are sisters of the boudoir forming poetry societies. I am not afraid that the begonias will be sung in the spring to the autumn of chrysanthemums. How can I understand the infinite sorrow in my heart. Suddenly, a word leaked the secret. I began to recognize their secret schemes. Thinking carefully, it really makes no sense. One is, paying respects to heaven and earth, they are married in harmony. One is, Xiao Xiang is windy and rainy, and the bamboo is rustling. They burn all the new poems and old handkerchiefs. They end a life like a flower. A daughter's body, the dream awakens in the Red Chamber.

Metropolitan Opera Society

Movies

Silver Jottings

— Zhi Er

After Yuan Muzhi went to Nanjing once, "it is said" that he is going to leave Diantong.

The reason for leaving Diantong, according to Yuan Muzhi's personal propaganda, Bao Ke "Pin", is that he could not stand Sun Shiyi's exclusion.

The day before yesterday, Bao Ke "Pin" took that propaganda draft to various newspapers to ask for publication, but as a result, when the newspapers called Diantong to inquire, the colleagues at Diantong were stunned. They said that they did not know that Ai Muzhi had resigned, and even did not know that Yuan Muzhi had the intention to resign.

If Yuan Muzhi really leaves Diantong, (in fact, he will never do so, this is clever propaganda, and also a trick of borrowing a knife to kill,) some say he will go to Japan, (it is said that boss Ma Dejian once said this. "If Muzhi goes to Japan, all expenses will be borne by him.") Some also say he will join Mingxing.

Joining Mingxing is unlikely, because we know that Mingxing already has Ying Yunwei there.

Some people wonder why Muzhi's relationship with his friends is so bad? Apart from Muzhi himself, probably only Zhao Bangfeng and Bao Ke knows.

Dangerous Moment

— Da Shanghai Movie Review

A Little Record of the Imperial Commissioner's Photography

That evening, the third movie show had already ended, but the upstairs of the Jin Cheng was still bustling with noise. It turned out that amateur actors were preparing to take costume stills of "Imperial Commissioner."

The actors were excitedly and playfully teasing each other, some were getting their hair permed, and some were trying on costumes. Most were lively and full of youthful energy. Only the two masters, Yang Jimin and Xin Hanwen, calmly handled their tools, one setting up the lights and adjusting the camera on the stage, and the other organizing makeup and rushing to make County Magistrate Gu Eryi's headgear upstairs.

Yin Xiucen and 　Mang were originally the Laurel and Hardy of the script. Lao Yin even thickened his nose on his big face, making him even more funny.

Shi Chao's makeup simply had a complete Russian flavor. That mustache, those dark circles around his eyes, that nose - on Avenue Joffre, one could often encounter people like him that night.

Lao Xin almost wanted to display his lifelong energy that night. There were really too many actors. Lao Xin carefully portrayed each actor's personality and features with oil paint and old brushes with great confidence.

Lao Yang initially had his wife helping him, but later it got late, so he was left to work alone. The director, Zhang Min, was a nice guy, lying under the stage directing the actors' poses.

Among the actors, Zheng Junli's makeup was the most successful, with almost the demeanor of Rasputin. Gu Eryi's appearance was the funniest. His stomach was stuffed with pillows to be almost as big as the fat guy Gu Xiucen, and he wore a newly made headgear on his head, with a round nose. As soon as he walked out of the dressing room, everyone was surprised and didn't recognize him.

That day, Jin Shan's makeup was really beautiful. His military uniform was straight, his face was covered with No. 2 oil paint, and he played with a monocle in his hand, truly a dandy young master.

Finally, Wang Ying and Ye Luxi went to be photographed. It was almost dawn. When Wang Ying walked off the stage, Lao Yang was sleeping on the sofa. Miss Wang urged, "Yang Little Sheep, hurry up and get up and take pictures with me! Oh, he's asleep, poor thing." Lao Yang, while organizing the dry plates, said, "Working so hard, taking photos all night, this is really the first time in my life."

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automotive Weekly

The United States Expands Automotive Manufacturing

Investing a Huge Sum of 100 Million Dollars

According to news from Detroit, the heart of the American automobile industry, major American automobile giants are now planning a grand and effective expansion plan, with the money they plan to spend reportedly reaching US$100,000,000. This is truly a considerable amount. Since 1919, until the recent years of economic decline, almost all industries were shrouded in the gloomy mist of depression. Not to mention an investment of such a huge amount, it is an unprecedented initiative in various industries since 1919. There are also many manufacturers that have been hit hard by the economy and have become unable to recover.

The aforementioned US$100,000,000 includes the total amount of funds earmarked in the expansion plans of major automobile factories. The majority of this amount is for: (1) the design and manufacture of new car models. This cost is not small, because each factory designs and manufactures new models every year. At this time, everyone is very competitive, and factories do not hesitate to spend a lot of money and recruit talent to do this important work. Now that autumn is over and winter has begun, it is the important season for each factory to compete and work hard to manufacture new car models. Several leading car factories have completed the manufacture of sample cars for the 1936 model year. Starting next month, they will be given to distributors for early viewing, as an aid in sales planning. It is said that there will be a preview exhibition in New York on November 2 for this purpose. Because of the manufacture of new car models, the factory's equipment and work will also be expanded and improved accordingly, naturally requiring a large amount of money to cope with.

(2) Restoring factories that have been closed. Many of the factories of major automobile manufacturers have been temporarily suspended in recent years due to the impact of market decline and economic shocks, resulting in contraction. Now that there is a glimmer of improvement in the market, and 1936 is just around the corner, everyone is excitedly focusing their efforts on work. As a result, several factories that have been closed for many years are planning to resume operations and start work again. This matter, in fact, will naturally cost a lot of money, such as purchasing tools, repairing factory buildings, and hiring workers, all of which require funds. Although the amount of $100,000,000 is large, with these two major expenditures, there is not much left.

This large investment of 100 million dollars is, needless to say, one of the largest expenditures of the two major giants in the American automobile industry - General Motors and Ford. The investment amount already planned by General Motors is US$50,000,000, and the factory expansion cost already announced by Ford is US$27,000,000. Some points in this plan are already underway. In addition, several million dollars will be used to purchase new tools to prepare for the manufacture of 1936 model cars.

People in the automobile industry have long said that they are, on the one hand, the first to be aware of economic panic, and on the other hand, the vanguard of resuming work. Therefore, in the years when the world economic recession struck, the automobile industry also suffered early, and now, it seems that there is a glimmer of recovery, so the automobile industry also has a sign of gradual prosperity. The weakest point of automobile buyers' purchasing power in recent years was in 1932. During this period, various factories made great efforts to tighten their belts, and all unnecessary expenditures were reduced in production. Therefore, the replacement and addition of tools and other items were also postponed. However, at the end of the year, looking at the balance sheet after the accounts were settled, it was still a loss. (Yu)

The Development History of Diesel Engines for Automobiles (4)

— Zhu Yisheng

Because of the excellent performance of diesel engines, various agricultural tractors are now mostly equipped with them. According to experience, the car oil consumed by a diesel engine tractor per day is less than the driver's daily food expenses.

Diesel engines have also made amazing developments in other various uses. Cranes, excavators, rock crushers, and air conditioners - more than 20 manufacturers are preparing to use diesel engines as the power source for their products. On the water, we can see that all kinds of ships, large and small, are equipped with diesel engines. Large passenger ships such as the Augustus, more than 700 feet long and with a displacement of 30,000 tons, which travel between Europe and the United States, are also equipped with diesel propulsion engines. Secondly, ships such as the Georgic and Britannic of the British Cunard Company, with a displacement of 27,000 tons each, are also equipped with diesel engines. Currently, almost 90% of oil tankers in the world are equipped with diesel engines.

The Shanghai French Concession Water and Electricity Plant has completely switched to diesel engines, and this is even more the case in cities in Europe and the United States. The large locks of the Panama Canal also use diesel engines to open and close. The crude oil gushing out of the mines is also transported in thousand-mile-long pipelines by using diesel engines to turn pumps to pour and transport it.

Currently, diesel engine manufacturers in Europe and the United States are realizing that this engine is becoming increasingly perfect and are engaged in standard manufacturing, which will reduce costs in the future on the one hand, and facilitate assembly on the other.

In aviation, the advantages of diesel engines are also very obvious. (1) Because of the economy of fuel consumption, it can carry more valuable weight. (2) Heavy oil is not easy to burn, which provides a major safety guarantee. (3) Gasoline engines are most prone to problems with spark plugs and carburetors, which diesel engines do not have. A few years ago, Packard Motor Car Company created a diesel aircraft engine with 225 horsepower and weighing 510 pounds, which was the first diesel engine for aircraft. Currently, various European and American powers are engaged in researching the structure of aircraft diesel engines, so that once the electrical death ray is completed, the electrical equipment used by gasoline engines will lose its effectiveness. Diesel engines, however, have no connection with electricity and cannot be affected by the death ray. Therefore, France is currently offering a reward of 1 million francs to anyone who can invent a diesel engine for aircraft that can be installed on a fighter and has the same speed as a gasoline engine.

Crossing the French border, we can see that the German Lurdentze Aviation Company is engaged in installing diesel engines on its transport aircraft. This aircraft will be the bomber in future wars. In a recent test flight, a Chumot-type diesel engine manufactured by a Yonggu factory could generate 650 horsepower at an altitude of 11,400 feet. Its weight per horsepower was 2.6 pounds. In addition, various factories such as British Sunlight, Italian Fiat, and French Claire also have commendable results in the testing of diesel aircraft engines.

Currently, a factory in the western United States has begun manufacturing a large diesel engine for aircraft. It is an inverted V-type twelve-cylinder water-cooled engine. Its planner is a Belgian engineer. Its horsepower can reach 1,200 horsepower.
